## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p04/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


M = 2048
K = 1048576
N = 1


@substrate.jit
def gemm_kernel(
    A: S.Tensor((2048, 1048576), S.bf16),
    B: S.Tensor((1048576, 1), S.bf16),
    C: S.Tensor((2048, 1), S.bf16),
):
    for i in S.range(M):
        for j in S.range(N):
            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for kk in S.range(K):
                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()

    def forward(self, A, B):
        if tuple(A.shape) != (2048, 1048576) or tuple(B.shape) != (1048576, 1):
            return torch.matmul(A, B)
        A = A.contiguous()
        B = B.contiguous()
        C = torch.empty((2048, 1), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
        return C

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_cuda_nvidia


@substrate.jit
def gemm_2stages_pipeline(
    A: S.Tensor((128, 128), S.f16),
    B: S.Tensor((128, 128), S.f16),
    C: S.Tensor((128, 128), S.f16),
):
    MMA_M = 16
    MMA_N = 8
    MMA_K = 16

    WARP_SIZE = 32

    # Work group configuration
    WARPS_M = 2  # Number of warps in M dimension per work group
    WARPS_N = 2  # Number of warps in N dimension per work group

    # Each warp computes multiple MMA tiles
    MMA_TILES_M = 2  # Number of MMA tiles per warp in M dimension
    MMA_TILES_N = 2  # Number of MMA tiles per warp in N dimension

    # Block size
    BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * MMA_TILES_M * MMA_M  # Total M covered by work group
    BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * MMA_TILES_N * MMA_N  # Total N covered by work group

    K_tiles = 8  # 128 // 16

    # =========================================== #

    # Work group and warp identification
    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N

    thread_id = S.thread_id(0)
    warp_id = thread_id >> 5  # thread_id // WARP_SIZE
    lane_id = thread_id % WARP_SIZE

    warp_row_id = warp_id >> 1  # warp_id // WARPS_N
    warp_col_id = warp_id % WARPS_N

    # Shared memory: [stage][warp_row][warp_col][local_row][local_col]
    # A: [2][WARPS_M][MMA_TILES_M][MMA_M][MMA_K]
    # B: [2][WARPS_N][MMA_TILES_N][MMA_N][MMA_K]
    a_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 2, 16, 16), S.f16)
    b_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 2, 8, 16), S.f16)
    c_smem = S.make_shared((2, 2, 2, 2, 16, 8), S.f16)

    # Accumulators for each MMA tile this warp computes
    RC = S.make_local((2, 2, 4), S.f16)

    for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
        for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
            for i in S.range(4):
                RC[tm, tn, i] = S.convert(0, S.f16)

    # Precompute addressing for A and B loads
    row_a = lane_id >> 1
    col_a = (lane_id & 1) * 8
    row_b = (lane_id % (MMA_N * 2)) >> 1
    col_b = ((lane_id % (MMA_N * 2)) & 1) * 8

    # Stage 0: Prefetch first tile (k_tile = 0) into buffer 0
    write_stage = 0
    for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
        for j in S.range(8):
            global_row = block_row + warp_row_id * (MMA_TILES_M * MMA_M) + tm * MMA_M + row_a
            global_col = col_a + j
            a_smem[write_stage, warp_row_id, tm, row_a, col_a + j] = A[global_row, global_col]

    for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
        for j in S.range(8):
            global_row = col_b + j
            global_col = block_col + warp_col_id * (MMA_TILES_N * MMA_N) + tn * MMA_N + row_b
            b_smem[write_stage, warp_col_id, tn, row_b, col_b + j] = B[global_row, global_col]

    S.syncthreads()

    # Main pipeline loop
    for k_tile in S.range(K_tiles - 1):
        read_stage = k_tile & 1
        write_stage = 1 - read_stage

        # Prefetch next tile
        next_k = k_tile + 1
        for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
            for j in S.range(8):
                global_row = block_row + warp_row_id * (MMA_TILES_M * MMA_M) + tm * MMA_M + row_a
                global_col = next_k * MMA_K + col_a + j
                a_smem[write_stage, warp_row_id, tm, row_a, col_a + j] = A[global_row, global_col]

        for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
            for j in S.range(8):
                global_row = next_k * MMA_K + col_b + j
                global_col = block_col + warp_col_id * (MMA_TILES_N * MMA_N) + tn * MMA_N + row_b
                b_smem[write_stage, warp_col_id, tn, row_b, col_b + j] = B[global_row, global_col]

        # Compute all MMA tiles for this warp
        for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
            for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
                # Load A tile
                a_row_offset = lane_id % 16
                a_col_offset = (lane_id >> 4) * 8
                a_smem_tile = S.subview(a_smem, (read_stage, warp_row_id, tm, 0, 0), (1, 1, 1, 16, 16), (1, 1, 1, 1, 1))
                a_tile_2d = S.subview(a_smem_tile, (a_row_offset, a_col_offset), (8, 8), (1, 1))
                RA = S.nvvm.ldmatrix_m8n8_x4_b16(a_tile_2d)

                # Load B tile
                b_row_offset = lane_id % 8
                b_col_offset = ((lane_id >> 3) & 1) * 8
                b_smem_tile = S.subview(b_smem, (read_stage, warp_col_id, tn, 0, 0), (1, 1, 1, 8, 16), (1, 1, 1, 1, 1))
                b_tile_2d = S.subview(b_smem_tile, (b_row_offset, b_col_offset), (8, 8), (1, 1))
                RB = S.nvvm.ldmatrix_m8n8_x2_b16(b_tile_2d)

                # MMA
                RC_view = S.subview(RC, (tm, tn, 0), (1, 1, 4), (1, 1, 1))
                RC_result = S.nvvm.mma_16x8x16_f16_f16(RA, RB, RC_view)

                # Store back to RC
                for i in S.range(4):
                    RC[tm, tn, i] = RC_result[i]

        S.syncthreads()

    # Handle the last k_tile
    last_stage = (K_tiles - 1) & 1

    for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
        for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
            # Load A tile
            a_row_offset = lane_id % 16
            a_col_offset = (lane_id >> 4) * 8
            a_smem_tile_last = S.subview(
                a_smem, (last_stage, warp_row_id, tm, 0, 0), (1, 1, 1, 16, 16), (1, 1, 1, 1, 1)
            )
            a_tile_2d_last = S.subview(a_smem_tile_last, (a_row_offset, a_col_offset), (8, 8), (1, 1))
            RA = S.nvvm.ldmatrix_m8n8_x4_b16(a_tile_2d_last)

            # Load B tile
            b_row_offset = lane_id % 8
            b_col_offset = ((lane_id >> 3) & 1) * 8
            b_smem_tile_last = S.subview(b_smem, (last_stage, warp_col_id, tn, 0, 0), (1, 1, 1, 8, 16), (1, 1, 1, 1, 1))
            b_tile_2d_last = S.subview(b_smem_tile_last, (b_row_offset, b_col_offset), (8, 8), (1, 1))
            RB = S.nvvm.ldmatrix_m8n8_x2_b16(b_tile_2d_last)

            # MMA
            RC_view = S.subview(RC, (tm, tn, 0), (1, 1, 4), (1, 1, 1))
            RC_result = S.nvvm.mma_16x8x16_f16_f16(RA, RB, RC_view)

            # Store back to RC
            for i in S.range(4):
                RC[tm, tn, i] = RC_result[i]

    S.syncthreads()

    # Store results to shared memory
    row1 = lane_id >> 2
    col1 = (lane_id & 3) * 2

    for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
        for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
            c_smem[warp_row_id, warp_col_id, tm, tn, row1, col1] = RC[tm, tn, 0]
            c_smem[warp_row_id, warp_col_id, tm, tn, row1, col1 + 1] = RC[tm, tn, 1]
            c_smem[warp_row_id, warp_col_id, tm, tn, row1 + 8, col1] = RC[tm, tn, 2]
            c_smem[warp_row_id, warp_col_id, tm, tn, row1 + 8, col1 + 1] = RC[tm, tn, 3]

    S.syncthreads()

    # Write results to global memory
    for tm in S.range(MMA_TILES_M):
        for tn in S.range(MMA_TILES_N):
            for j in S.range(MMA_N):
                global_row = block_row + warp_row_id * (MMA_TILES_M * MMA_M) + tm * MMA_M + (lane_id % MMA_M)
                global_col = block_col + warp_col_id * (MMA_TILES_N * MMA_N) + tn * MMA_N + j
                C[global_row, global_col] = c_smem[warp_row_id, warp_col_id, tm, tn, (lane_id % MMA_M), j]


@unittest.skipUnless(
    has_cuda_nvidia(),
    "Requires CUDA with an NVIDIA GPU.",
)
class TestGEMM(unittest.TestCase):
    def setUp(self):
        """Set up test fixtures before each test method."""
        torch.manual_seed(0)
        self.M = 128
        self.N = 128
        self.K = 128
        self.rtol = 1e-1
        self.atol = 1e-1

    def test_gemm_2stage(self):
        """[NVVM] Test 2-stage GEMM with float16 precision using MMA intrinsics."""
        A = torch.randn((self.M, self.K), dtype=torch.float16, device="cuda")
        B = torch.randn((self.K, self.N), dtype=torch.float16, device="cuda")
        C = torch.zeros((self.M, self.N), dtype=torch.float16, device="cuda")

        expected = (A @ B).to(dtype=torch.float16, device="cpu")

        WARPS_M = 2
        WARPS_N = 2
        MMA_TILES_M = 2
        MMA_TILES_N = 2
        MMA_M = 16
        MMA_N = 8

        BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * MMA_TILES_M * MMA_M  # 2 * 2 * 16 = 64
        BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * MMA_TILES_N * MMA_N  # 2 * 2 * 8 = 32

        grid_x = (self.N + BLOCK_N - 1) // BLOCK_N
        grid_y = (self.M + BLOCK_M - 1) // BLOCK_M

        gemm_2stages_pipeline[lambda: ((grid_x, grid_y, 1), (WARPS_M * WARPS_N * 32, 1, 1))](A, B, C)

        actual = C.to("cpu")

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.allclose(actual, expected, rtol=self.rtol, atol=self.atol),
            msg=f"GEMM results do not match.\nExpected:\n{expected}\nActual:\n{actual}\n"
            f"Max absolute difference: {torch.max(torch.abs(actual - expected))}",
        )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
import _substrate_bindings as _C
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip(
    src: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    dst: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)
    dst_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(dst, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    offset_x2 = S.convert(4, S.i32)
    offset_x4 = S.convert(12, S.i32)

    value_x1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x1(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    value_x2 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x2(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    value_x4 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)

    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x1(value_x1, dst_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x2(value_x2, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x4(value_x4, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view(
    src: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    dst: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    frag = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    for i in S.range(2):
        for j in S.range(4):
            dst[i * 4 + j] = frag[i, j, 0]


def generate_mlir(jit_fn) -> str:
    jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(jit_fn)
    import_module = _build_import_module([jit_fn, *jit_deps])

    generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
    generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)

    for dep in jit_deps:
        dep_func = _get_function_def(dep.parse())
        generator.visit_function_def(dep_func, "[]", "jit")

    kernel_func = _get_function_def(jit_fn.parse())
    generator.visit_function_def(kernel_func, "[]", "kernel")
    return generator.get_mlir()


@unittest.skipUnless(
    has_rocm(),
    "Requires ROCm/HIP with an AMD GPU.",
)
class TestAMDGPUBufferOps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_raw_buffer_roundtrip(self):
        src = torch.arange(7, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 - 9
        dst = torch.full((7,), -1, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_make_rsrc_generates_pointer_and_range(self):
        mlir = generate_mlir(kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip)

        self.assertIn(
            "substrate.memref.extract_aligned_pointer_as_index",
            mlir,
        )
        self.assertGreaterEqual(mlir.count("vector.insert %arg2"), 2, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_load"), 3, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_store"), 3, mlir)

    def test_raw_buffer_bf16_view_extract(self):
        src = torch.randn((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        dst = torch.zeros((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

import torch
import substrate
import substrate.language as S

@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32), B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32), C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32)):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)
    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    C[lane] = c_lane

def pack_row_major_A(mat):
    # 32x8 bf16 -> 64x2 u32, lane l maps row=l//2, col4=(l%2)*4
    out = torch.zeros((64,2), dtype=torch.uint32)
    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32,8)
    for l in range(64):
        r = l//2
        c0 = (l%2)*4
        for j in range(2):
            lo = int(vals[r,c0+2*j].item())
            hi = int(vals[r,c0+2*j+1].item())
            out[l,j] = lo | (hi<<16)
    return out

def pack_row_major_B(mat):
    # 8x32 bf16 -> 64x2 u32, lane l maps row=l//8, col4=(l%8)*4 ??? 8 frags/row impossible with 2 u32=4 bf16. actually 32 cols => 8 fragments.
    out = torch.zeros((64,2), dtype=torch.uint32)
    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8,32)
    for l in range(64):
        r = l//8
        frag = l%8
        c0 = frag*4
        for j in range(2):
            lo = int(vals[r,c0+2*j].item())
            hi = int(vals[r,c0+2*j+1].item())
            out[l,j] = lo | (hi<<16)
    return out

if not torch.cuda.is_available():
    raise SystemExit('no cuda')

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 2
+        col0 = (lane % 2) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.zeros((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    A[0, 0] = 1
+    B[0, 0] = 1
+    Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+    Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+    C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+    gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+    nz = (C.cpu() == 1).nonzero()
+    print(nz)
+    print("sum", C.sum().item(), "max", C.max().item())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 2
+        col0 = (lane % 2) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.zeros((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    A[0, 0] = 1
+    B[0, 0] = 1
+    Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+    Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+    C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+    gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+    nz = (C.cpu() == 1).nonzero()
+    print(nz)
+    print("sum", C.sum().item(), "max", C.max().item())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 2
+        col0 = (lane % 2) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    samples = [(0, 0), (1, 0), (2, 0), (15, 0), (16, 0), (17, 0), (0, 1), (0, 2), (0, 15), (0, 16), (0, 17), (31, 31)]
+    for row, col in samples:
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.zeros((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1

+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)

+        nz = (C.cpu() == 1).nonzero()
+        print((row, col), nz.tolist())
+

+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 2
+        col0 = (lane % 2) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    samples = [(0, col) for col in range(32)]
+    for row, col in samples:
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.zeros((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        B[0, col] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        nz = (C.cpu() == 1).nonzero()
+        if nz.numel():
+            print((row, col), nz.tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

index 0000000000000000000000000000000000000000..1e2eba92202f49580e194b291087c4c45d6b9541
--- /dev/null
+++ b/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p04/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/mfma_probe.py
@@ -0,0 +1,66 @@
+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 2
+        col0 = (lane % 2) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    samples = [(0, col) for col in range(32)]
+    for row, col in samples:
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.zeros((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        B[0, col] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        nz = (C.cpu() == 1).nonzero()
+        if nz.numel():
+            print((row, col), nz.tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

exec

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 2
+        col0 = (lane % 2) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 2
+        col0 = (lane % 2) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

codex
I found the issue: the naive row-major A fragment packing aliases rows `0..15` and `16..31`. I’m switching the probe to a more plausible 16-row interleaved lane mapping and then I’ll lock that into the kernel.

/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p04/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/mfma_probe.py
diff --git a/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p04/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/mfma_probe.py b/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p04/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/mfma_probe.py
new file mode 100644
index 0000000000000000000000000000000000000000..ac0bfa08a813950e46a7abc1b235c40ded431c74
--- /dev/null
+++ b/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p04/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/mfma_probe.py
@@ -0,0 +1,64 @@
+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = (lane % 16) + 16 * (lane // 32)
+        col0 = ((lane // 16) % 2) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane

+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)

+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)

+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)

+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),

+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE

+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N

+    a_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)

+

+        if tid < WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:

+            a_row = block_row + (a_frag % 32)

+            a_offset = S.convert((a_row * K + a_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_a = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):

+

+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

+        b_words = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        a_idx = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+

+            b_words[i] = b_smem[b_idx, i]
+

+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+

+        S.syncthreads()
+

+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + 4 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8

+            or self._cached_b_ptr != B.data_ptr()

+            self._cached_b_ptr = B.data_ptr()

+            self._cached_b_tiled is None
+            or self._cached_b_ptr != B.data_ptr()
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.device != B.device
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.dtype != B.dtype
+        ):
+            B_tiled = torch.empty((K, B_PADDED_N), device=B.device, dtype=B.dtype)
+            grid = ((K + 255) // 256, 1, 1)
+            pack_b_kernel[lambda: (grid, (256, 1, 1))](B, B_tiled)

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * 32
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * 32
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARPS_M * WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE

+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    block_row = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // WARPS_N
+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_tiled, b_range_bytes)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // K_TILE):
+        if tid < WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            a_frag = tid
+            a_row = block_row + (a_frag % 32)
+            a_k = k_tile * K_TILE + (a_frag // 32) * 8
+            a_offset = S.convert((a_row * K + a_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_a = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[a_frag, i] = packed_a[i]
+
+        if tid >= WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            b_frag = tid - WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE
+            b_row = k_tile * K_TILE + (b_frag // 8)
+            b_col = (b_frag % 8) * 8
+            b_offset = S.convert((b_row * B_PADDED_N + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_b = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                b_smem[b_frag, i] = packed_b[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        b_words = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        a_idx = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_words[i] = a_smem[a_idx, i]
+            b_words[i] = b_smem[b_idx, i]
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        if lane == 32:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + 4 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8

index 0000000000000000000000000000000000000000..653049c55bfbef5f7d9c30a4d6619430d63212db

@@ -0,0 +1,64 @@
+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * 32

+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    block_row = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // WARPS_N
+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_tiled, b_range_bytes)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // K_TILE):
+        if tid < WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            a_frag = tid
+            a_row = block_row + (a_frag % 32)
+            a_k = k_tile * K_TILE + (a_frag // 32) * 8
+            a_offset = S.convert((a_row * K + a_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_a = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[a_frag, i] = packed_a[i]
+
+        if tid >= WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            b_frag = tid - WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE
+            b_row = k_tile * K_TILE + (b_frag // 8)
+            b_col = (b_frag % 8) * 8
+            b_offset = S.convert((b_row * B_PADDED_N + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_b = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                b_smem[b_frag, i] = packed_b[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        b_words = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        a_idx = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_words[i] = a_smem[a_idx, i]
+            b_words[i] = b_smem[b_idx, i]
+

+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)

+

+++ b/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p04/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/mfma_probe.py

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    block_row = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // WARPS_N
+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_tiled, b_range_bytes)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // K_TILE):
+        if tid < WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            a_frag = tid
+            a_row = block_row + (a_frag % 32)
+            a_k = k_tile * K_TILE + (a_frag // 32) * 8
+            a_offset = S.convert((a_row * K + a_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_a = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[a_frag, i] = packed_a[i]
+
+        if tid >= WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            b_frag = tid - WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE
+            b_row = k_tile * K_TILE + (b_frag // 8)
+            b_col = (b_frag % 8) * 8
+            b_offset = S.convert((b_row * B_PADDED_N + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_b = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                b_smem[b_frag, i] = packed_b[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        b_words = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        a_idx = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_words[i] = a_smem[a_idx, i]
+            b_words[i] = b_smem[b_idx, i]
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

+                if row < M:

The failing construct is the local `u32` buffer feeding MFMA. I’m changing that to a value-style vector initialization so the MFMA operands match the working example more closely.

+++ b/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p04/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/mfma_probe.py

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

 K = 1048576
 N = 1
 
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * 32
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * 32
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARPS_M * WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE
+K_TILE = 16
+B_PADDED_N = BLOCK_N
+
 
 @substrate.jit
-def gemm_kernel(
-    A: S.Tensor((2048, 1048576), S.bf16),
-    B: S.Tensor((1048576, 1), S.bf16),
-    C: S.Tensor((2048, 1), S.bf16),
+def pack_b_kernel(
+    B: S.Tensor((K, 1), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
 ):
-    for i in S.range(M):
-        for j in S.range(N):
-            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for kk in S.range(K):
-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)
+    idx = S.block_id(0) * S.block_dim(0) + S.thread_id(0)
+    if idx < K:
+        value = B[idx, 0]
+        for col in S.range(B_PADDED_N):
+            B_tiled[idx, col] = value
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    block_row = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // WARPS_N
+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_tiled, b_range_bytes)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // K_TILE):
+        if tid < WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            a_frag = tid
+            a_row = block_row + (a_frag % 32)
+            a_k = k_tile * K_TILE + (a_frag // 32) * 8
+            a_offset = S.convert((a_row * K + a_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_a = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[a_frag, i] = packed_a[i]
+
+        if tid >= WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            b_frag = tid - WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE
+            b_row = k_tile * K_TILE + (b_frag // 8)
+            b_col = (b_frag % 8) * 8
+            b_offset = S.convert((b_row * B_PADDED_N + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_b = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                b_smem[b_frag, i] = packed_b[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        b_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        a_idx = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_words[i] = a_smem[a_idx, i]
+            b_words[i] = b_smem[b_idx, i]
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    if warp_col == 0:
+        if lane == 0:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        if lane == 32:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + 4 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
 
 
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._cached_b_ptr = None
+        self._cached_b_tiled = None
 
+    def _get_b_tiled(self, B: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        if (
+            self._cached_b_tiled is None
+            or self._cached_b_ptr != B.data_ptr()
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.device != B.device
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.dtype != B.dtype

         return C

+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),

+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+

+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+def gemv_mfma_kernel(

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,

+    tid = S.thread_id(0)

+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // WARPS_N
+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N
+

+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)

+

+            a_row = block_row + (a_frag % 32)

+            for i in S.range(4):

+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+import torch

+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S

+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(

+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),

+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+

+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):

+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):

+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out

+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * 32
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * 32
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARPS_M * WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE

+        for col in S.range(B_PADDED_N):

+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    block_row = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // WARPS_N
+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_tiled, b_range_bytes)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // K_TILE):
+        if tid < WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            a_frag = tid
+            a_row = block_row + (a_frag % 32)
+            a_k = k_tile * K_TILE + (a_frag // 32) * 8
+            a_offset = S.convert((a_row * K + a_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_a = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[a_frag, i] = packed_a[i]
+
+        if tid >= WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            b_frag = tid - WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE
+            b_row = k_tile * K_TILE + (b_frag // 8)
+            b_col = (b_frag % 8) * 8
+            b_offset = S.convert((b_row * B_PADDED_N + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_b = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                b_smem[b_frag, i] = packed_b[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_idx = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[a_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[b_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    if warp_col == 0:
+        if lane == 0:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        if lane == 32:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + 4 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._cached_b_ptr = None
+        self._cached_b_tiled = None
 
+    def _get_b_tiled(self, B: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        if (
+            self._cached_b_tiled is None
+            or self._cached_b_ptr != B.data_ptr()
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.device != B.device
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.dtype != B.dtype
+        ):
+            B_tiled = torch.empty((K, B_PADDED_N), device=B.device, dtype=B.dtype)
+            grid = ((K + 255) // 256, 1, 1)
+            pack_b_kernel[lambda: (grid, (256, 1, 1))](B, B_tiled)
+            self._cached_b_ptr = B.data_ptr()
+            self._cached_b_tiled = B_tiled
+        return self._cached_b_tiled
+
     def forward(self, A, B):

+            raise ValueError(f"Expected A {(M, K)} and B {(K, 1)}, got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}")
+

         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((2048, 1), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)

+        C = torch.empty((M, 1), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+
+        a_range_bytes = A.numel() * A.element_size()
+        b_range_bytes = B_tiled.numel() * B_tiled.element_size()
+        grid = (M // BLOCK_M, 1, 1)
+        gemv_mfma_kernel[lambda: (grid, (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B_tiled, C, a_range_bytes, b_range_bytes)
         return C

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
 ):
-    for i in S.range(M):
-        for j in S.range(N):
-            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for kk in S.range(K):
-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)
+    idx = S.block_id(0) * S.block_dim(0) + S.thread_id(0)
+    if idx < K:
+        value = B[idx, 0]
+        for col in S.range(B_PADDED_N):
+            B_tiled[idx, col] = value
 
 
+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    block_row = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // WARPS_N
+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_tiled, b_range_bytes)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // K_TILE):
+        if tid < WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            a_frag = tid
+            a_row = block_row + (a_frag % 32)
+            a_k = k_tile * K_TILE + (a_frag // 32) * 8
+            a_offset = S.convert((a_row * K + a_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_a = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[a_frag, i] = packed_a[i]
+
+        if tid >= WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            b_frag = tid - WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE
+            b_row = k_tile * K_TILE + (b_frag // 8)
+            b_col = (b_frag % 8) * 8
+            b_offset = S.convert((b_row * B_PADDED_N + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_b = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                b_smem[b_frag, i] = packed_b[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_idx = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[a_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[b_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    if warp_col == 0:
+        if lane == 0:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        if lane == 32:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + 4 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._cached_b_ptr = None
+        self._cached_b_tiled = None
 
+    def _get_b_tiled(self, B: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        if (
+            self._cached_b_tiled is None
+            or self._cached_b_ptr != B.data_ptr()
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.device != B.device
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.dtype != B.dtype
+        ):
+            B_tiled = torch.empty((K, B_PADDED_N), device=B.device, dtype=B.dtype)
+            grid = ((K + 255) // 256, 1, 1)
+            pack_b_kernel[lambda: (grid, (256, 1, 1))](B, B_tiled)
+            self._cached_b_ptr = B.data_ptr()
+            self._cached_b_tiled = B_tiled
+        return self._cached_b_tiled

-            return torch.matmul(A, B)

+
+        a_range_bytes = A.numel() * A.element_size()
+        b_range_bytes = B_tiled.numel() * B_tiled.element_size()
+        grid = (M // BLOCK_M, 1, 1)
+        gemv_mfma_kernel[lambda: (grid, (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B_tiled, C, a_range_bytes, b_range_bytes)
         return C

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()
