+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)

+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),
+    a_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    b_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    block_row = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // WARPS_N
+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range_bytes)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_tiled, b_range_bytes)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // K_TILE):
+        if tid < WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            a_frag = tid
+            a_row = block_row + (a_frag % 32)
+            a_k = k_tile * K_TILE + (a_frag // 32) * 8
+            a_offset = S.convert((a_row * K + a_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_a = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[a_frag, i] = packed_a[i]
+
+        if tid >= WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            b_frag = tid - WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE
+            b_row = k_tile * K_TILE + (b_frag // 8)
+            b_col = (b_frag % 8) * 8
+            b_offset = S.convert((b_row * B_PADDED_N + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_b = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):

+        S.syncthreads()
+

+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[a_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[b_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

+                if row < M:

     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._cached_b_ptr = None

+    def _get_b_tiled(self, B: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:

codex
The runtime failure is a descriptor-range overflow on the 4 GB A tensor. I’m fixing that by building the A buffer resource from a 64-row subview per block so the descriptor stays under the 32-bit range limit.
apply patch

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+        for col in S.range(B_PADDED_N):
+            B_tiled[idx, col] = value
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_row = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // WARPS_N
+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_block = S.subview(A, (block_row, 0), (BLOCK_M, K), (1, 1))
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_block, BLOCK_M * K * 2)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_tiled, K * B_PADDED_N * 2)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // K_TILE):
+        if tid < WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            a_frag = tid
+            a_row = a_frag % 32
+            a_k = k_tile * K_TILE + (a_frag // 32) * 8
+            a_offset = S.convert((a_row * K + a_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_a = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[a_frag, i] = packed_a[i]
+
+        if tid >= WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            b_frag = tid - WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE
+            b_row = k_tile * K_TILE + (b_frag // 8)
+            b_col = (b_frag % 8) * 8
+            b_offset = S.convert((b_row * B_PADDED_N + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_b = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                b_smem[b_frag, i] = packed_b[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
 
+        a_idx = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[a_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[b_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
 
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    if warp_col == 0:
+        if lane == 0:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        if lane == 32:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + 4 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._cached_b_ptr = None
+        self._cached_b_tiled = None
+
+    def _get_b_tiled(self, B: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        if (
+            self._cached_b_tiled is None
+            or self._cached_b_ptr != B.data_ptr()
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.device != B.device
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.dtype != B.dtype
+        ):
+            B_tiled = torch.empty((K, B_PADDED_N), device=B.device, dtype=B.dtype)
+            grid = ((K + 255) // 256, 1, 1)
+            pack_b_kernel[lambda: (grid, (256, 1, 1))](B, B_tiled)
+            self._cached_b_ptr = B.data_ptr()
+            self._cached_b_tiled = B_tiled
+        return self._cached_b_tiled
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (2048, 1048576) or tuple(B.shape) != (1048576, 1):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
+        if tuple(A.shape) != (M, K) or tuple(B.shape) != (K, 1):
+            raise ValueError(f"Expected A {(M, K)} and B {(K, 1)}, got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}")
+
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((2048, 1), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        B_tiled = self._get_b_tiled(B)
+        C = torch.empty((M, 1), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+
+        grid = (M // BLOCK_M, 1, 1)
+        gemv_mfma_kernel[lambda: (grid, (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B_tiled, C)
         return C

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+            packed_b = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                b_smem[b_frag, i] = packed_b[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
 
+        a_idx = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[a_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[b_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
 
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    if warp_col == 0:
+        if lane == 0:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        if lane == 32:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + 4 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._cached_b_ptr = None
+        self._cached_b_tiled = None
+
+    def _get_b_tiled(self, B: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        if (
+            self._cached_b_tiled is None
+            or self._cached_b_ptr != B.data_ptr()
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.device != B.device
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.dtype != B.dtype

+            grid = ((K + 255) // 256, 1, 1)
+            pack_b_kernel[lambda: (grid, (256, 1, 1))](B, B_tiled)
+            self._cached_b_ptr = B.data_ptr()
+            self._cached_b_tiled = B_tiled
+        return self._cached_b_tiled

         return C

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * 32

+def gemv_mfma_kernel(

+

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * 32
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARPS_M * WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE

+    idx = S.block_id(0) * S.block_dim(0) + S.thread_id(0)

+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_row = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)

+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // WARPS_N
+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+

+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_tiled, K * B_PADDED_N * 2)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+

+        if tid < WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            a_frag = tid
+            a_row = a_frag % 32

+            a_offset = S.convert((a_row * K + a_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_a = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)

+

+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[b_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

diff --git a/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p04/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/mfma_probe.py b/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p04/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/mfma_probe.py

+++ b/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p04/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/mfma_probe.py
@@ -0,0 +1,64 @@
+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    C[lane] = c_lane
+
+
+def pack_a(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(32, 8)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane % 32
+        col0 = (lane // 32) * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def pack_b(mat):
+    vals = mat.view(torch.uint16).view(8, 32)
+    out = torch.zeros((64, 2), dtype=torch.uint32)
+    for lane in range(64):
+        row = lane // 8
+        frag = lane % 8
+        col0 = frag * 4
+        for j in range(2):
+            lo = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j].item())
+            hi = int(vals[row, col0 + 2 * j + 1].item())
+            out[lane, j] = lo | (hi << 16)
+    return out
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    for row in range(32):
+        A = torch.zeros((32, 8), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        B = torch.ones((8, 32), dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        A[row, 0] = 1
+        Ap = pack_a(A).to(device)
+        Bp = pack_b(B).to(device)
+        C = torch.zeros((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
+        gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](Ap, Bp, C)
+        Ccpu = C.cpu()
+        nz = (Ccpu.abs() > 0.5).nonzero()
+        print(row, "sum", Ccpu.sum().item(), "nz0", nz[:8].tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

 K = 1048576
 N = 1
 
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WARPS_M = 2
+WARPS_N = 2
+BLOCK_M = WARPS_M * 32
+BLOCK_N = WARPS_N * 32
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARPS_M * WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE
+K_TILE = 16
+B_PADDED_N = BLOCK_N
+
 
 @substrate.jit
-def gemm_kernel(
-    A: S.Tensor((2048, 1048576), S.bf16),
-    B: S.Tensor((1048576, 1), S.bf16),
-    C: S.Tensor((2048, 1), S.bf16),
+def pack_b_kernel(
+    B: S.Tensor((K, 1), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
 ):
-    for i in S.range(M):
-        for j in S.range(N):
-            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for kk in S.range(K):
-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)
+    idx = S.block_id(0) * S.block_dim(0) + S.thread_id(0)
+    if idx < K:
+        value = B[idx, 0]
+        for col in S.range(B_PADDED_N):
+            B_tiled[idx, col] = value
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_row = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // WARPS_N
+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_block = S.subview(A, (block_row, 0), (BLOCK_M, K), (1, 1))
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_block, BLOCK_M * K * 2)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_tiled, K * B_PADDED_N * 2)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // K_TILE):
+        if tid < WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            a_frag = tid
+            a_row = a_frag % 32
+            a_k = k_tile * K_TILE + (a_frag // 32) * 8
+            a_offset = S.convert((a_row * K + a_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_a = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[a_frag, i] = packed_a[i]
+
+        if tid >= WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            b_frag = tid - WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE
+            b_row = k_tile * K_TILE + (b_frag // 8)
+            b_col = (b_frag % 8) * 8
+            b_offset = S.convert((b_row * B_PADDED_N + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_b = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                b_smem[b_frag, i] = packed_b[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
 
+        a_idx = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[a_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[b_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
 
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    if warp_col == 0:
+        if lane == 0:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        if lane == 32:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + 4 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._cached_b_ptr = None
+        self._cached_b_tiled = None
+
+    def _get_b_tiled(self, B: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        if (
+            self._cached_b_tiled is None
+            or self._cached_b_ptr != B.data_ptr()
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.device != B.device
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.dtype != B.dtype
+        ):
+            B_tiled = torch.empty((K, B_PADDED_N), device=B.device, dtype=B.dtype)
+            grid = ((K + 255) // 256, 1, 1)
+            pack_b_kernel[lambda: (grid, (256, 1, 1))](B, B_tiled)
+            self._cached_b_ptr = B.data_ptr()
+            self._cached_b_tiled = B_tiled
+        return self._cached_b_tiled
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (2048, 1048576) or tuple(B.shape) != (1048576, 1):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
+        if tuple(A.shape) != (M, K) or tuple(B.shape) != (K, 1):
+            raise ValueError(f"Expected A {(M, K)} and B {(K, 1)}, got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}")

         B = B.contiguous()

+@substrate.jit
+def gemv_mfma_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16),
+    B_tiled: S.Tensor((K, B_PADDED_N), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M, 1), S.bf16),
+):
+    block_row = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_M
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // WARPS_N
+    warp_col = warp_id % WARPS_N
+
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((WARPS_N * WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_block = S.subview(A, (block_row, 0), (BLOCK_M, K), (1, 1))
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_block, BLOCK_M * K * 2)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_tiled, K * B_PADDED_N * 2)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // K_TILE):
+        if tid < WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            a_frag = tid
+            a_row = a_frag % 32
+            a_k = k_tile * K_TILE + (a_frag // 32) * 8
+            a_offset = S.convert((a_row * K + a_k) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_a = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[a_frag, i] = packed_a[i]
+
+        if tid >= WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE:
+            b_frag = tid - WARPS_M * WAVE_SIZE
+            b_row = k_tile * K_TILE + (b_frag // 8)
+            b_col = (b_frag % 8) * 8
+            b_offset = S.convert((b_row * B_PADDED_N + b_col) * 2, S.i32)
+            packed_b = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                b_smem[b_frag, i] = packed_b[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
 
+        a_idx = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        b_idx = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+        a_frag = S.view(a_smem[a_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_smem[b_idx], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
 
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    if warp_col == 0:
+        if lane == 0:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+        if lane == 32:
+            for i in S.range(16):
+                row = block_row + warp_row * 32 + 4 + (i % 4) + (i // 4) * 8
+                if row < M:
+                    C[row, 0] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._cached_b_ptr = None
+        self._cached_b_tiled = None
+
+    def _get_b_tiled(self, B: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        if (
+            self._cached_b_tiled is None
+            or self._cached_b_ptr != B.data_ptr()
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.device != B.device
+            or self._cached_b_tiled.dtype != B.dtype
+        ):
+            B_tiled = torch.empty((K, B_PADDED_N), device=B.device, dtype=B.dtype)
+            grid = ((K + 255) // 256, 1, 1)
+            pack_b_kernel[lambda: (grid, (256, 1, 1))](B, B_tiled)
+            self._cached_b_ptr = B.data_ptr()
+            self._cached_b_tiled = B_tiled
+        return self._cached_b_tiled
 
     def forward(self, A, B):

-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
+        if tuple(A.shape) != (M, K) or tuple(B.shape) != (K, 1):
+            raise ValueError(f"Expected A {(M, K)} and B {(K, 1)}, got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}")
+

         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((2048, 1), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        B_tiled = self._get_b_tiled(B)
+        C = torch.empty((M, 1), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+
+        grid = (M // BLOCK_M, 1, 1)
+        gemv_mfma_kernel[lambda: (grid, (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B_tiled, C)
         return C
